\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The {\ttfamily Fuel\+Entry\+Model} defines the data required and stored for a fuel purchase made through Load Master. 

This class provides a means for a driver to store critical information about each fuel purchase as a means of maintaining a history of fuel purchases and understanding how driving conditions, speeds, etc., affect fuel economy. By having all of this information stored in the Fuel Account Journal, {\ttfamily 10040.\+jrnl}, the driver will be able to make informed decisions regarding his/her driving practices in order to reduce their fuel expense over time.

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Sean Carrick $<$sean at pekinsoft dot com$>$
\end{DoxyAuthor}

The trip number with which this model is associated. 

The value returned will either be the trip that was active at the time this transaction occurred, or the phrase "No Active Load".

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setDate()}{setDate()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void com.\+pekinsoft.\+loadmaster.\+model.\+Fuel\+Purchase\+Model.\+set\+Date (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Date}]{date }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the purchase date for this fuel entry as a {\ttfamily java.\+util.\+Date} object. 


\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[Note]The date is created as the current date by default when a new {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1pekinsoft_1_1loadmaster_1_1model_1_1FuelPurchaseModel}{Fuel\+Purchase\+Model}}} is created. This setter may be used for adding the date to the object when reading records from a data file, or when entering a fuel purchase at a date later than when it was purchased.
\end{DoxyDescription}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em date} & the purchase date. \\

\index{com.pekinsoft.loadmaster.model.FuelPurchaseModel@{com.pekinsoft.loadmaster.model.FuelPurchaseModel}!setDate@{setDate}}
\index{setDate@{setDate}!com.pekinsoft.loadmaster.model.FuelPurchaseModel@{com.pekinsoft.loadmaster.model.FuelPurchaseModel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setDate()}{setDate()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void com.\+pekinsoft.\+loadmaster.\+model.\+Fuel\+Purchase\+Model.\+set\+Date (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Date}]{date }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the purchase date for this fuel entry as a {\ttfamily java.\+util.\+Date} object. 


\begin{DoxyDescription}
\item[Note]The date is created as the current date by default when a new {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1pekinsoft_1_1loadmaster_1_1model_1_1FuelPurchaseModel}{Fuel\+Purchase\+Model}}} is created. This setter may be used for adding the date to the object when reading records from a data file, or when entering a fuel purchase at a date later than when it was purchased.
\end{DoxyDescription}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em date} & the purchase date. \\
